	writefile_2();
	if (!is_file('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php') != 'bffa15f8793fa4236f60573432c3b72370253e20') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php') !== 'bffa15f8793fa4236f60573432c3b72370253e20') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php') !== '0152e0e7d0bd054362697a687b61e5b139ec2c57') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_2();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php') !== 'bffa15f8793fa4236f60573432c3b72370253e20') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php');
		}
	}

		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php') != 'd2656561e837eb34825d3e07dce8fa0320ded1fc') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php');
	}

	if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php') !== 'd2656561e837eb34825d3e07dce8fa0320ded1fc') {

			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_3();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php') !== 'd2656561e837eb34825d3e07dce8fa0320ded1fc') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php');

if (!is_file('plugins/objectTypes/oid/plugin.inc.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/objectTypes/oid/plugin.inc.php');
	writefile_8();
	if (!is_file('plugins/objectTypes/oid/plugin.inc.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/objectTypes/oid/plugin.inc.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/objectTypes/oid/plugin.inc.php') != '31bb34bea7fd28415339dda834627b1bb37a8810') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/objectTypes/oid/plugin.inc.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/objectTypes/oid/plugin.inc.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/objectTypes/oid/plugin.inc.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/objectTypes/oid/plugin.inc.php') !== '31bb34bea7fd28415339dda834627b1bb37a8810') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/objectTypes/oid/plugin.inc.php') !== 'c9beebe7450cfa5083b4cd22e42fc2234b881472') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/objectTypes/oid/plugin.inc.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/objectTypes/oid/plugin.inc.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/objectTypes/oid/plugin.inc.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/objectTypes/oid/plugin.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_8();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/objectTypes/oid/plugin.inc.php') !== '31bb34bea7fd28415339dda834627b1bb37a8810') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/objectTypes/oid/plugin.inc.php');
		}
	}
}


file_put_contents('oidplus_version.txt', "Revision 228\n");
